 Cosy+ devices running a firmware 21.x below 21.2s10 or a firmware 22.x below 22.1s3 are vulnerable to code injection due to improper parameter blacklisting. This is fixed in version 21.2s10 and 22.1s3.

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2023-42470
 The Imou Life com.mm.android.smartlifeiot application through 6.8.0 for Android allows Remote Code Execution via a crafted intent to an exported component. This relates to the com.mm.android.easy4ip.MainActivity activity. JavaScript execution is enabled in the WebView, and direct web content loading occurs.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools.  In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. ## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-33896
 Cosy+ devices running a firmware 21.x below 21.2s10 or a firmware 22.x below 22.1s3 are vulnerable to code injection due to improper parameter blacklisting. This is fixed in version 21.2s10 and 22.1s3.

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2023-42470
 The Imou Life com.mm.android.smartlifeiot application through 6.8.0 for Android allows Remote Code Execution via a crafted intent to an exported component. This relates to the com.mm.android.easy4ip.MainActivity activity. JavaScript execution is enabled in the WebView, and direct web content loading occurs.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. ## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). ## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2023-51385
 In ssh in OpenSSH before 9.6, OS command injection might occur if a user name or host name has shell metacharacters, and this name is referenced by an expansion token in certain situations. For example, an untrusted Git repository can have a submodule with shell metacharacters in a user name or host name.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

 The Imou Life com.mm.android.smartlifeiot application through 6.8.0 for Android allows Remote Code Execution via a crafted intent to an exported component. This relates to the com.mm.android.easy4ip.MainActivity activity. JavaScript execution is enabled in the WebView, and direct web content loading occurs.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

This relates to the com.mm.android.easy4ip.MainActivity activity. JavaScript execution is enabled in the WebView, and direct web content loading occurs.

## CVE-2020-2733
 Vulnerability in the JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools product of Oracle JD Edwards (component: Monitoring and Diagnostics). The supported version that is affected is 9.2. Easily exploitable vulnerability allows unauthenticated attacker with network access via HTTP to compromise JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. Successful attacks of this vulnerability can result in takeover of JD Edwards EnterpriseOne Tools. CVSS 3.0 Base Score 9.8 (Confidentiality, Integrity and Availability impacts). CVSS Vector: (CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:N/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:H/A:H).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z

## CVE-2024-22120
 Zabbix server can perform command execution for configured scripts. After command is executed, audit entry is added to "Audit Log". Due to "clientip" field is not sanitized, it is possible to injection SQL into "clientip" and exploit time based blind SQL injection.

## CVE-2024-3183
 A vulnerability was found in FreeIPA in a way when a Kerberos TGS-REQ is encrypted using the clients session key. This key is different for each new session, which protects it from brute force attacks. However, the ticket it contains is encrypted using the target principal key directly. For user principals, this key is a hash of a public per-principal randomly-generated salt and the users password.If a principal is compromised it means the attacker would be able to retrieve tickets encrypted to any principal, all of them being encrypted by their own key directly. By taking these tickets and salts offline, the attacker could run brute force attacks to find character strings able to decrypt tickets when combined to a principal salt (i.e. find the principals password).

- [https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC](https://github.com/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC) :  
![starts](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
![forks](https://img.shields.io/github/forks/Cyxow/CVE-2024-3183-POC.svg) 
2024-08-20T14:16:04Z
